“appropriate officer”, in relation to any functions to be performed under this Act, means the officer of Customs to whom such functions have been assigned by or under this Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6[ (bb) “Bangladesh customs-waters” means the waters extending into the sea to a distance of twelve nautical miles measured from the appropriate base line on the coast of Bangladesh;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[ (c) “bill of entry” means a bill of entry delivered under section 79, and includes, an electronically transmitted bill of entry in such cases and in such manner containing such particulars as the Board may specify;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8[ (d) “bill of export” means a bill of export delivered under section 131, and includes an electronically transmitted bill of export in such cases and in such manner containing such particulars as the Board may specify;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9[ (e) “Board” means the National Board of Revenue constituted under the National Board of Revenue Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 76 of 1972);]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) “coastal goods” means goods transported in a vessel from one port in Bangladesh to another, but does not include imported goods on which customs-duty has not been paid;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10[ (ff) “container” means a receptacle of permanent nature, having an internal volume of one metre or more, fully or partially enclosed to constitute a compartment for containing goods and specially designed to facilitate carriage of goods by one or more modes of transport, without intermediate reloading, and ready handling, particularly when transferred from one mode of transport to another and strong enough for repeated use;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(fff) “controlling authority”, in relation to any customs-airport, customs-port, customs-inland container depot or customs-station, means the owner or legal occupier thereof or any person having legal control thereof;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g) “conveyance” means any means of transport used for carrying goods or passengers such as a vessel, aircraft, vehicle or animal;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h) “customs-airport” means any airport declared under section 9 to be a customs-airport;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) “customs-area” means the limits of the customs-station specified under section 10 and includes any area in which imported goods or goods for export are ordinarily kept before clearance by the customs authorities;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">11[ (ii) “Customs computer system” means the customs computerised entry processing system established by the Board for the purposes of this Act;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">12[ (iii) “customs-inland container depot” means any place declared under section 9 to be a customs-inland container depot;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(j) “customs-port” means any place declared under section 9 to be a port for the shipment and landing of goods;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(k) “customs-station” means any customs-port, customs-airport or any land customs-station;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">13[ (kk) “export manifest” means an export manifest delivered under section 53, and includes an electronically transmitted export manifest in such cases and in such manner containing such particulars as the Board may specify;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(l) “goods” means all movable goods and includes-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) conveyances,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) stores and materials,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">14[ (iii) baggage,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv) currency and negotiable instruments,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(v) electronic data.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">15[ (ll) “import manifest” means an import manifest delivered under sections 43 and 44, and includes an electronically transmitted import manifest in such cases and in such manner containing such particulars as the Board may specify;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(m) “land customs-station” means any place including an inland river port declared under section 9 to be a land customs-station;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(n) “master” when used in relation to any vessel, means any person, except a pilot or harbour master, having command or charge of such vessel;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(o) “officer of Customs” means an officer appointed under section 3;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">16[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">17[ (pp) “person” includes a company, partnership, association, firm or a body of persons;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(q) “person-in-charge” means-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) in relation to a vessel, the master of the vessel;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) in relation to an aircraft, the commander or pilot in charge of the aircraft;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii) in relation to a railway train, the conductor, guard or other person having the chief direction of the train;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv) in relation to any other conveyance, the driver or any other person having control of the conveyance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">18[ (qq) “pre-shipment inspection agency” means any person appointed under section 25A as a pre-shipment inspection agency and includes a representative of that person;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">19[ (qqa) “prescribed” means prescribed by rules or order, as the case may be;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">20[ (qqq) “registered user”, in relation to a Customs computer system, means a user of that system and registered for the purposes of this Act;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(r) “rules” means the rules made under this Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">21[ (s) “smuggle” means to bring into or take out of Bangladesh in breach of any prohibition or restriction for the time being in force; or evading payment of customs-duties or taxes leviable thereon,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) narcotics, narcotic drugs or psychotropic substance; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) gold bullion, silver bullion, platinum, palladium, radium, precious stones, currency, manufactures of gold or silver or platinum or palladium or precious stones, or any other goods notified by the Government in the official Gazette, in each case exceeding22[ Taka ten lakhs] in value; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) any goods concealed in any manner in any place on board any ship, vessel or aircraft or in any other vehicle or in any baggage or cargo or on person; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) any other goods by any route other than a route declared under section 9 or 10 from any place other than a customs-station; and includes an attempt, abetment or connivance of so bringing in or taking out of such goods; and all cognate words and expressions shall be construed accordingly;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">23[ 24[ (t) “special bonded warehouse” means a private warehouse licensed under section 13 and which is a hundred percent export oriented industry to be determined as such by the Board for the purpose of exemption from the provision of sub-section (2) of section 91;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(tt) “warehouse” means of place appointed under section 12 or a place licensed under section 13;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(u) “warehousing station” means a place declared as a warehousing station under section 11;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(v) “wharf ” means any place in customs-port approved under clause (b) of section 10 for the loading and unloading of goods or any class of goods.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER II</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">APPOINTMENT OF OFFICERS OF CUSTOMS AND THEIR POWERS</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appointment of officers of Customs                  25[ 3. For the purposes of this Act, the Board may, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint, in relation to any area or function specified in the notification, any person to be-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) a Commissioner of Customs;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) a Commissioner of Customs (Appeal);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) a Commissioner of Customs (Bond);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) a Commissioner of Customs (Valuation and Internal Audit);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) a Director General (Customs Intelligence and Investigation);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">26[ (f) a Director General (Audit, Intelligence and Investigation, Value Added Tax);]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g) a Director General (Duty Exemption and Drawback);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h) a Director General (Training);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">27[ (hh) a Director General, Central Intelligence Cell;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">28[ (i) an Additional Commissioner of Customs or an Additional Director General;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">29[ (j) a Joint Commissioner of Customs or a Director;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(k) a Deputy Commissioner of Customs or a Deputy Director;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(l) an Assistant Commissioner of Customs or an Assistant Director;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">30[ (ll) a Revenue Officer;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(m) an officer of Customs with any other designation.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Powers and duties of officers of Customs                      4. An officer of Customs appointed under section 3 shall exercise such powers and discharge such duties as are conferred or imposed on him by or under this Act; and he shall also be competent to exercise all powers and discharge all duties conferred or imposed upon any officer subordinate to him:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that, notwithstanding anything contained in this Act or the rules, the Board may, by general or special order, impose such limitations or conditions on the exercise of such powers and discharge of such duties as it thinks fit.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Delegation of powers                31[ 5. The Board may, by notification in the official Gazette, and subject to such limitations or conditions, if any, as may be specified therein, empower by name or designation-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">32[ (a) any Additional Commissioner of Customs to exercise any of the powers of a Commissioner of Customs specified in clauses (a), (b), (c) and (d) of section 3;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) any Joint Commissioner of Customs to exercise any of the powers of an Additional Commissioner of Customs or a Commissioner of Customs 33[ specified at clauses (a), (c) and (d) of section 3];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) any Deputy Commissioner of Customs to exercise any of the powers of a Joint Commissioner of Customs or an Additional Commissioner of Customs;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) any Assistant Commissioner of Customs to exercise any of the powers of a Deputy Commissioner of Customs;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) any other officer of Customs to exercise any of the powers of an Assistant Commissioner of Customs.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Entrustment of functions of the Customs officers to certain other officers             6. The Board may, by notification in the official Gazette, entrust, either conditionally or unconditionally, any functions of any officer of Customs under this Act to any officer of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Assistance to the officers of Customs                34[ 7. Assistance to the officers of customs.- All officers and staffs of government and semi-government organizations, law enforcement agencies, security forces, autonomous bodies, statutory bodies, financial institutions, educational institutions, private organizations, local government and non-government organizations shall assist the officers of customs in the discharge of their functions under this Act.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Exemption from service on jury or inquest or as assessors                      8. Notwithstanding anything contained in any other law, no officer of the Board or Commissioner of Customs and no other officer of Customs whom the Board or Commissioner of Customs deems it necessary to exempt on grounds of public duty, shall be compelled to serve on 35[ an inquest].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER III</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">DECLARATION OF PORTS, AIRPORTS, LAND CUSTOMS- STATIONS, ETC.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Declaration of customs-ports, customs-airports, etc                   9. The Board may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the ports and airports which alone shall be customs-ports or customs-airports for the unloading of imported goods and loading of goods for export or any class of such goods;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the places which alone shall be land customs-stations 36[ or customs-inland container depot] for the clearance of goods or any class of goods imported or to be exported by land or inland waterways;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the routes by which alone goods or any class of goods specified in the notification may pass by land or inland waterways into or out of Bangladesh, or to or from any land customs-station or to or from any land frontier;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) the places which alone shall be ports for the carrying on of coastal trade with any specified customs-ports in Bangladesh; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) what shall for the purposes of this Act be deemed to be a custom-house and the limits thereof.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to approve landing places and specify limits of customs-stations              10. The Board may, by notification in the official Gazette-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) specify the limits of any customs-station; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) approve proper places in any customs-station for the loading and unloading of goods or any class of goods.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to declare warehousing stations              11. The Board may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare places to be warehousing stations at which alone public warehouses may be appointed and private warehouses may be licensed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to appoint public warehouses                 12. At any warehousing station, the 37[ Commissioner of Customs (Bond) or any other Commissioner of Customs authorised by the Board] may, from time to time, appoint public warehouses wherein dutiable goods may be deposited without payment of customs-duty.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Licensing of Private warehouses                        38[ 13. (1) Subject to sub-section (2), at any warehousing station, the Commissioner of Customs (Bond) or any other Commissioner of Customs authorised by the Board may, license private warehouses wherein dutiable goods imported by or on behalf of the licensee, or any other imported goods in respect of which facilities for deposit in a public warehouse are not available, may be deposited.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Board may, from time to time, by notification in the official Gazette, impose conditions, limitations or restrictions-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) on granting licence for private warehouse;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) on goods to be warehoused; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) on import entitlement of the warehouse.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Commissioner of Customs (Bond) or any other Commissioner of Customs authorised by the Board may, suspend or cancel a licence granted under sub-section (1)-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) if the licensee contravenes any provision of this Act or the rules made thereunder or commits breach of any of the conditions of the licence; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) in the case where, he deems fit, a license to be suspended or cancelled in the public interest:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that in case of cancellation of any licence, the licensee shall be served with a show cause notice of thirty days, and be given a reasonable opportunity of being heard.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Stations for officers of Customs to board and land                     14. The Commissioner of Customs may, from time to time, appoint, in or near any customs-ports, stations or limits at or within which vessels arriving at or departing from such port shall bring to for the boarding or landing of officers of customs, and may, unless separate provisions therefore have been made under the Ports Act, 1908 (XV of 1908) direct at what particular place in any such port vessels, not brought into port by pilots, shall anchor or moor.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER IV</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">PROHIBITION AND RESTRICTION OF IMPORTATION AND EXPORTATION</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Prohibitions                  15. No goods specified in the following clauses shall be brought, whether by air or land or sea, into Bangladesh:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) counterfeit coin;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) forged or counterfeit currency notes;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) any obscene book, pamphlet, paper, drawing, painting, representation, figure, photograph, film or article;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) goods having applied thereto a counterfeit trade mark within the meaning of the39[ Penal Code] (Act XLV of 1860), or a false trade description within the meaning of the Merchandise Marks Act, 1889 (IV of 1889);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) goods made or produced outside Bangladesh and having applied thereto any name or trade mark, being or purporting to be the name or trade mark of any manufacturer, dealer or trader in Bangladesh unless-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) the name or trade mark is, as to every application thereof, accompanied by a definite indication of the goods having been made or produced in a place outside Bangladesh; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) the country in which that place is situated is in that indication shown in letters as large and conspicuous as any letter in the name or trade mark, and in the same language and character as the name or trade mark;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) piece-goods manufactured outside Bangladesh (such as are ordinarily sold by length or by the piece), unless the real length thereof in standard 40[ metres] or other measurement for the time being applying in Bangladesh has been conspicuously stamped on each piece in Arabic numerals; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g) goods made or produced outside Bangladesh and intended for sale, and having applied thereto, a design in which copy-right exists under the Patents And Designs Act, 1911 (II of 1911) in respect of the class to which the goods belong or any fraudulent or obvious imitation of such design except when the application of such design has been made with the licence or written consent of the registered proprietor of the design:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">41[ Provided that the Government may, by an order in writing, condone, subject to such conditions, limitations or restrictions, if any, as it thinks fit to impose, any classes of goods from the provisions mentioned in sub-section (d), (e), (f) and (g).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to prohibit or restrict importation and exportation of goods                     16. The Government may, from time to time, by notification in the official Gazette, prohibit or restrict the bringing in to or taking out of Bangladesh of any goods of specified description by air, sea or land.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Detention and confiscation of goods imported in breach of section 15 or section 16                    42[ 17. Where any goods are imported into or attempted to be exported out of Bangladesh in violation of the provisions of the section 15 or of a notification under section 16, such goods shall, without prejudice to any other penalty to which the offender may be liable under this Act, or any other law, be liable to be detained and confiscated and shall be disposed of in such a manner as may be prescribed.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER V</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">LEVY OF, EXEMPTION FROM AND REPAYMENT OF, CUSTOMS-DUTIES</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Goods dutiable             43[ 18. (1) Except as hereinafter provided, customs-duties shall be levied at such rates as are prescribed in the First Schedule 44[ * * *] or under any other law for the time being in force on</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) goods imported into, or exported from, Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) goods brought from any foreign country to any customs-station, and without payment of duty there, transhipped or transported for, or thence carried to, and imported at, any other customs station; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) goods brought in bond from one customs station to another 45[ :</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that no customs-duty under this Act or other tax leviable by a Customs officer under any other law for the time being in force shall be levied or collected in respect thereof, if-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) in value of the goods in any one consignment do not exceed one thousand Taka; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the total amount of such duty and tax does not exceed Taka one thousand.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">46[ (2) The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, levy, subject to such conditions, limitations or restrictions as it may deem fit to impose, a regulatory duty on all or any of the goods specified in the First Schedule at the rate not exceeding the highest rate of customs-duty 47[ * * *] specified in the said Schedule.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">48[ Explanation.- The rate of regulatory duty on any such goods may be higher than that of the customs-duty leviable on that goods as prescribed in the said Schedule, provided such regulatory duty does not exceed the highest rate of customs-duty of that Schedule.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The regulatory duty levied under sub section (2) shall be in addition to any duty imposed under sub section (1) or under any other law for the time being in force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Any notification issued under sub section (2) shall, if not earlier rescinded, stand rescinded on the expiry of the financial year in which it was issued.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) and (6) [Added by section 5 of A_© AvBb, 1993 (1993 m‡bi 18 bs AvBb) and subsequently omitted by section 5 of A_© AvBb, 1995 (1995 m‡bi 12 bs AvBb).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Imposition of countervailing duty                       49[ 18A. (1) Where any country or territory pays, bestows, directly or indirectly, any subsidy upon the manufacture or production therein or the exportation therefrom of any goods including any subsidy on transportation of such goods, then, upon the importation of any such goods into Bangladesh, whether the same is imported directly from the country of manufacture, production or otherwise, and whether it is imported in the same condition as when exported from the country of manufacture or production or has been changed in condition by manufacture, production or otherwise, the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, impose a countervailing duty not exceeding the amount of such subsidy.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Explanation.- For the purposes of this section, subsidy shall be deemed to exist, if-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) there is financial contribution by a Government, or any public body within the territory of the exporting or producing country, that is, where-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) a Government practice involves a direct transfer of funds (including grants, loans and equity infusion) or potential direct transfer of funds or liabilities or both;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) Government revenue that is otherwise due is forgone or not collected (including fiscal incentives);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii) a Government provides goods or services other than general infrastructure or purchases goods;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv) a Government makes payments to funding mechanism, or entrusts or directs a private body to carry out one or more of the type of functions specified in clauses (i), (ii) and (iii) which would normally be vested in the Government and the practice, in no real sense, differs from practices normally followed by Governments; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) a Government grants or maintains any form of income or price support, which operates directly or indirectly to increase export of any goods from, or to reduce import of any goods to its territory, and a benefit is thereby conferred.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Government may, pending the determination of the amount of subsidy, in accordance with the provisions of this section and the rules made thereunder impose a countervailing duty under this sub-section not exceeding the amount of such subsidy as provisionally estimated by it and if such countervailing duty exceeds the subsidy as so determined,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the Government shall, having regard to such determination and as soon as may be after such determination reduce such countervailing duty; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) refund shall be made of so much of such countervailing duty which has been collected as is in excess of the countervailing duty as so reduced.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Subject to any rules made by the Government, by notification in the official Gazette, the countervailing duty under sub-section (1) or sub-section (2) shall not be levied unless it is determined that-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the subsidy relates to export performance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the subsidy relates to the use of domestic raw materials over imported raw materials in the exported goods; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the subsidy has been conferred on a limited number of persons engaged in manufacturing, producing or exporting the goods unless such a subsidy is for-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) research activities conducted by or on behalf of persons engaged in the manufacture, production or export; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) assistance to disadvantaged regions within the territory of the exporting country; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii) assistance to promote adaptation of existing facilities to new environmental requirements.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) If the Government, is of the opinion that the injury to the domestic industry which is difficult to repair, is caused by massive imports in a relatively short period, of the goods benefiting from subsidies paid or bestowed and where in order to preclude the recurrence of such injury, it is necessary to levy countervailing duty retrospectively, the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, impose countervailing duty from a date prior to the date of imposition of countervailing duty under sub-section (2) but not beyond ninety days from the date of notification under that sub-section and notwithstanding anything contained in any law for the time being in force, such duty shall be payable from the date as specified in the notification issued under this sub-section.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The countervailing duty chargeable under this section shall be in addition to any other duty imposed under this Act or any other law for the time being in force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) The countervailing duty imposed under this section shall unless revoked earlier, cease to have effect on the expiry of five years from the date of such imposition:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that if the Government, in a review, is of the opinion that the cessation of such duty is likely to lead to continuation or recurrence of subsidisation and injury, it may, from time to time, extend the period of such imposition for a further period of five years and such further period shall commence from the date of order of such extension:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided further that where a review initiated before the expiry of the aforesaid period of five years has not come to a conclusion before such expiry, the countervailing duty may continue to remain in force pending outcome of such a review for a further period not exceeding one year.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7) The amount of any subsidy referred to in sub-section (1) or sub-section (2) shall, from time to time, be ascertained and determined by the Government, after such inquiry as it may consider necessary and the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for the identification of such goods and for the assessment and collection of any countervailing duty imposed upon the importation thereof under this section.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(8) No proceeding for imposition of countervailing duty under this section shall commence unless the Bangladesh Tariff Commission, on receipt of a written application by or on behalf of a domestic industry, informs the Government that there is prima-facie evidence of injury which is caused by direct or indirect subsidy on any particular imported goods.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Imposition of anti-dumping duty                        18B. (1) Where any goods are exported from any country or territory (hereinafter in this section referred to as the exporting country or territory) to Bangladesh at less than the normal value, then, upon the importation of such goods into Bangladesh, the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, impose an anti-dumping duty not exceeding the margin of dumping in relation to such goods.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Explanation.- For the purposes of this section,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) “margin of dumping”, in relation to any goods, means the difference between its export price and its normal value;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) “export price”, in relation to any goods, means the price of the goods exported from the exporting country or territory and in cases where there is no export price or where the export price is unreliable because of association or a compensatory arrangement between the exporter and the importer or a third party, the export price may be constructed on the basis of the price at which the imported goods are first resold to an independent buyer, or if the goods are not resold to an independent buyer, or not resold in the condition as imported, on such reasonable basis as may be determined in accordance with the rules made under sub-section (6);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) “normal value”, in relation to any goods, means-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) the comparable price, in the ordinary course of trade, for the like goods when meant for consumption in the exporting country or territory as determined in accordance with the rules made under sub-section (6); or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) when there are no sales of the like goods in the ordinary course of trade in the domestic market of the exporting country or territory, or, when because of the particular market situation or low volume of the sales in the domestic market of the exporting country or territory, such sales do not permit a proper comparison, the normal value shall be either-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) comparable representative price of the like goods when exported from the exporting country or territory or an appropriate third country as determined in accordance with the rules made under sub-section (6); or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the cost of production of the said goods in the country of origin along with reasonable addition for administrative, selling and general costs and for profits, as determined in accordance with the rules made under sub-section (6):</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that in the case of import of the goods from a country other than the country of origin and where the goods have been merely transhipped through the country of export or such goods are not produced in the country of export, or there is no comparable price in the country of export, the normal value shall be determined with reference to the price in country of origin.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Government may, pending the determination of the normal value and the margin of dumping in relation to any goods, in accordance with the provisions of this section and the rules made thereunder, impose on the importation of such goods into Bangladesh an anti-dumping duty on the basis of a provisional estimate of such value and margin and if such anti-dumping duty exceeds the margin as so determined-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the Government shall, having regard to such determination and as soon as may be after such determination, reduce such anti-dumping duty; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) refund shall be made of so much of the anti-dumping duty which has been collected as is in excess of anti-dumping duty as so reduced.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) if the Government, in respect of the dumped goods under inquiry, is of the opinion that-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) there is a history of dumping which caused injury or that the importer was, or should have been, aware that the exporter practices dumping and that such dumping cause injury; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) the injury is caused by massive dumping of goods imported in a relatively short time which in light of the timing and the volume of imported goods dumped and other circumstances, is likely to seriously undermine the remedial effect of the anti-dumping duty liable to be levied, the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, levy anti-dumping duty retrospectively from a date prior to the date of imposition of anti-dumping duty under sub-section (2) but not beyond ninety days from the date of notification under that sub-section and notwithstanding anything contained in any law for the time being in force, such duty shall be payable at such rate and from such date as may be specified in the notification.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) The anti-dumping duty chargeable under this section shall be in addition to any other duty imposed under this Act or any other law for the time being in force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The anti-dumping duty imposed under this section shall, unless revoked earlier, cease to have effect on the expiry of five years from the date of such imposition:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that if the Government, in a review, is of the opinion that the cessation of such duty is likely to lead to continuation or recurrence of dumping and injury, it may, from time to time, extend the period of such imposition for a further period of five years and such further period shall commence from the date of order of such extension:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided further that where a review initiated before the expiry of the aforesaid period of five years has not come to a conclusion before such expiry, the anti-dumping duty may continue to remain in force pending the outcome of such a review for a further period not exceeding one year.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) The margin of dumping as referred to in sub-section (1) or sub-section (2) shall, from time to time, as ascertained and determined by the Government after such inquiry as it may consider necessary and the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for the purposes of this section and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing, such rules may provide for the manner in which goods liable for any anti-dumping duty under this section may be identified and for the manner in which the export price and the normal value of and the margin of dumping in relation to such goods may be determined and for the assessment and collection of such anti-dumping duty.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7) No proceeding for imposition of anti-dumping duty under this section shall commence unless the Bangladesh Tariff Commission, on receipt of a written application by or on behalf of a domestic industry, informs the Government that there is prima-facie evidence of injury which is caused by dumping on any particular imported goods.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">No imposition under section 18A or 18B in certain cases                       18C. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained in section 18A or section 18B-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) no goods shall be subjected to both countervailing duty and anti-dumping duty to compensate for the same situation of dumping or export subsidisation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) The Government shall not levy any countervailing duty or anti-dumping duty-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) under section 18A or section 18B by reasons of exemption of such goods from duties or taxes borne by the like goods when meant for consumption in the country of origin or exportation or by reasons of refund of such duties or taxes;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) under sub-section (1) of each of these sections, on the import into Bangladesh of any goods from a member country of the World Trade Organization or from a country with which the Government of the People's Republic of Bangladesh has a most favoured nation agreement (hereinafter referred as a specified country), unless in accordance with the rules made under sub-section (2) of this section, a determination has been made that import of such goods into Bangladesh causes or threatens to cause material injury to any established industry in Bangladesh or materially retards the establishment of any industry in Bangladesh; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii) under sub-section (2) of each of these sections on import into Bangladesh of any goods from the specified countries unless in accordance with the rules made under sub-section (2) of this section, preliminary findings have been made of subsidy or dumping and consequent injury to domestic industry; and a further determination has also been made that a duty is necessary to prevent injury being caused during the investigation:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that nothing contained in sub-clauses (ii) and (iii) of clause (b) shall apply if a countervailing duty or an anti-dumping duty has been imposed on any goods to prevent injury or threat of an injury to the domestic industry of a third country exporting the like goods to Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) The Government may not levy-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) any countervailing duty under section 18A, at any time, upon receipt of satisfactory voluntary undertaking from the Government of the exporting country or territory agreeing to eliminate or limit the subsidy or take other measures concerning its effect, or the exporter agreeing to revise the price of the goods and if the Government is satisfied that injurious effect of the subsidy is eliminated thereby;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) any anti-dumping duty under section 18B, at any time upon receipt of satisfactory voluntary undertaking from any exporter to revise its prices or to cease exports to the area in question at dumped price and if the Government is satisfied that the injurious effect of dumping is eliminated by such action.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for the purposes of this section, and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing, such rules may provide for the manner in which any investigation may be made for the purposes of this section, the factors to which regard shall be paid in any such investigation and for all matters connected with such investigation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appeal against imposition of countervailing or anti-dumping duty                        18D. (1) An appeal against the order of determination or review thereof regarding the existence, degree and effect of any subsidy or dumping in relation to import of any goods shall lie to the Customs, Excise and ????? ?????? ?? Appellate Tribunal constituted under section 196.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Every appeal under this section shall be filed within ninety days of the date of order under appeal:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Appellate Tribunal may entertain any appeal after the expiry of the said period of ninety days, if it is satisfied that the appellant was prevented by sufficient cause from filing the appeal in time.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Appellate Tribunal may, after giving the parties to the appeal, an opportunity of being heard, pass such orders thereon as it thinks fit, confirming, modifying or annulling the order appealed against.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Every appeal under sub-section (1) shall be heard by a special Bench constituted by the President of the Appellate Tribunal for hearing such appeals and such Bench shall consist of the President and not less than two members and shall include one technical member and one judicial member.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p popular-posts="" style="text                      &lt;/div&gt;                    &lt;/div&gt;                  &lt;/article&gt;                                    &lt;div class=" widget="" widget_categories=""></p><h3 class="widget-title"><span>Disclaimer:</span></h3><div class="widget-content" style="text-align:justify;"><p>The information contains in this web-site is prepared for educational purpose. 345	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE DEFENCE SERVICES (INQUIRY) (SPECIAL PROVISIONS) ORDINANCE, 1969 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE DEFENCE SERVICES (INQUIRY) (SPECIAL PROVISIONS) ORDINANCE, 1969 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ORDINANCE NO. XIX OF 1969).[22nd July, 1969]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to make provision for a uniform procedure for inquiring into the conduct of a member of a Defence Service serving otherwise than in an organisation or unit of his service.     1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to make provision for a uniform procedure for inquiring into the conduct of a member of a Defence Service serving otherwise than in an organisation or unit of his service and for matters ancillary thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the 25th day of March, 1969, read with the Provisional Constitution Order, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the President is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the Defence Services (Inquiry) (Special Provisions) Ordinance, 1969.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It shall come into force on such date as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) “board of inquiry” means a board of inquiry convened under this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2[ (b)    “Chief of Staff,” in relation to a person whose conduct is inquired into under this Ordinance, means the Chief of Army Staff, Naval Staff or Air Staff, as the case may be;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “commanding officer”, in relation to a person subject to this Ordinance, means the head of the organisation or the commanding officer for the purpose of the service law of the unit in or to which such person is for the time being serving or attached;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        “service law”, in relation to a person whose conduct is inquired into under this Ordinance, means the 3[ * * *] Army Act, 1952 (XXXIX of 1952), the 4[ * * *] Air Force Act, 1953 (VI of 1953), or the 5[ * * *] Navy Ordinance, 1961 (XXXV of 1961), to which such person is subject;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) “unit” includes a naval ship, vessel or establishment of which there is a commanding officer for the purposes of the 6[ * * *] Navy Ordinance, 1961(XXXV of 1961).</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Inquiry into the conduct of certain persons subject to service law</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. The conduct of a person subject to a service law shall, notwithstanding anything contained in such law, be inquired into by a board of inquiry in accordance with the provisions of this Ordinance and the rules made thereunder where the conduct to be inquired into-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) relates to a period when he was serving or attached, except on secondment, in or to an organisation or unit other than that of the service to which he belongs, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        is that of such person together with that of another person who was not, during the period to which the conduct relates, subject to the same service law.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Convening of board of inquiry</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. Where the conduct to be inquired into under section 3 is that of the commanding officer or that of the commanding officer together with the conduct of another person, a board of inquiry shall be convened by the Chief of Staff 7[ * * *] to which the commanding officer belongs and, in any other case, by the commanding officer.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Composition of a board of inquiry, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) A board of inquiry shall consist of a president and such other persons and be convened in such manner, and the inquiry shall be conducted in accordance with such procedure, as may be prescribed by rules.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The president of a board of inquiry shall, after the conclusion of the inquiry, submit to the authority convening the board the proceedings of the board along with its findings and recommendations.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Upon the receipt of the proceedings of a board of inquiry submitted to him under sub-section (2), the commanding officer shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        if the inquiry relates to any matter which he is himself competent to dispose of, take the necessary action and forward a copy of the proceedings to the Chief of Staff, informing him of the action taken by him;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        if the inquiry relates to a matter which is not of the nature mentioned in clause (a), forward the proceedings together with his recommendations, to the Chief of Staff.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Upon the receipt of the proceedings of a board of inquiry submitted to him under sub-section (2), or forwarded to him under clause (b) of sub-section (3), the Chief of Staff shall direct that the person to whom the proceedings relate be dealt with in the manner authorised by the service law.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) For the purpose of taking any action under the service law, the proceedings of a board of inquiry convened under this Ordinance may be acted upon as if they were proceedings of a board of inquiry or Court of inquiry assembled under such law.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing power, such rules may provide for all or any of the following matters, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        the composition of a board of inquiry;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the manner of convening a board of inquiry;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the procedure for the conduct of inquiry; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) such other matters as may be necessary for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance the words “Government” and “Chief of Staff ” were substituted for the words “Central Government” and “Commander-in-Chief ” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 Clause (b) was substituted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The words “of the service” were omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
346	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE EX-GOVERNMENT SERVANTS (EMPLOYMENT WITH FOREIGN GOVERNMENTS) (PROHIBITION) ACT, 1966 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE EX-GOVERNMENT SERVANTS (EMPLOYMENT WITH FOREIGN GOVERNMENTS) (PROHIBITION) ACT, 1966 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ACT NO. XII OF 1966).[7th July, 1966]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Act to prohibit ex-Government servants from seeking or taking up employment with a foreign Government or foreign agency.  1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS in the interest of the security of Bangladesh, it is expedient to prohibit ex-Government servants from seeking or taking up employment with a foreign Government or foreign agency;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS the national interest in relation to the security of Bangladesh requires Central legislation in the matter under clause (2) of Article 131 of the Constitution;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Act may be called the Ex-Government Servants (Employment with Foreign Governments) (Prohibition) Act, 1966.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) “ex-Government servant” means any person who was, at any time, appointed or employed as an officer or 2[ employee of the Government] and has ceased to be so appointed or employed;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “foreign agency” means any office or establishment of the diplomatic or consular representative of a foreign Government by whatever name called, and includes any information, public relations, trade or commercial agency, service centre or foundation established or maintained by any such Government or by any person who is a national of a foreign country; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “foreign Government” means the Government of a foreign country.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Prohibition of employment, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) No ex-Government servant shall, except with the previous permission in writing of the 3[ Government], seek or take up employment as an officer or servant of a foreign Government or a foreign agency.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) [Omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalty</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. Whoever contravenes the provisions of section 3 shall be punishable with imprisonment for a term which may extend to one year, or with fine which may extend to five thousand 4[ Taka], or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Act, the word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the word “Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “employee of the Government” were substituted for the words “servant of the Central Government or a Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “Taka” was substituted for the word “rupees” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
347	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE EXCISE DUTY ON MINERALS (LABOUR WELFARE) ACT, 1967</h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE EXCISE DUTY ON MINERALS (LABOUR WELFARE) ACT, 1967 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ACT NO.
