</strong><strong>LANDS</strong><strong> AND BUILDINGS (RECOVERY OF POSSESSION) ORDINANCE, 1970 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE XXIV OF 1970).[18th September, 1970]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to repeal and with certain amendments, re-enact the East Bengal Government Lands and Buildings (Recovery of Possession) Act, 1952, and the East Pakistan Government Land (Unauthorised Occupation) Ordinance, 1960, and to consolidate the law relating to recovery of possession and assessment and recovery of compensation and arrear rent from unauthorised occupants of Government and Local Authority lands and buildings.             1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to repeal, and with certain amendments, re-enact the East Bengal Government Lands and Buildings (Recovery of Possession) Act, 1952, and the East Pakistan Government Land (Unauthorised Occupation) Ordinance, 1960, and to consolidate the law relating to recovery of possession and assessment and recovery of compensation and arrear rent from unauthorised occupants of Government and Local Authority lands and buildings;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the 25th day of March, 1969, read with the Provisional Constitution Order, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the Governor is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 2[ * * *] Government and Local Authority  Lands and Buildings (Recovery of Possession) Ordinance, 1970.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) This Ordinance, in so far as it relates to Government lands and buildings, shall come into force at once; and the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, extend it to such Local Authority and from such date as may be specified in the notification.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) “building” means a building which vests in, or is owned by, or is in possession or under the management and control of, the Government or a Local Authority, and includes the land appurtenant thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “Deputy Commissioner” means the Deputy Commissioner of a District and includes an Additional Deputy Commissioner or a Joint Deputy Commissioner and such other persons as may be appointed by the Government to perform all or any of the functions of a Deputy Commissioner under this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “land” means any land which vests in, or is owned by, or is in the possession or under the management and control of, the Government or Local Authority and includes any water;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        “Local Authority” means a local authority as defined in 3[ clause (28) of section 3 of the General Clauses Act, 1897 (X of 1897)];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        “prescribed” means prescribed by rules made by the Government under this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         “unauthorised occupant” means a person who is in occupation of any land or building or part thereof without having obtained the express permission or authority of the Government or the Local Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">concerned, as the case may be, and without executing, where necessary, a legal document, and includes-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) a person unlawfully inducted into any land or building or part thereof by the lessee; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) a lessee who continues in possession of the land or building or part thereof after expiry of term or determination of lease; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g) the words “lease” and “lessee” have the same meanings as in the Transfer of Property Act, 1882, and the word “lessee” includes his heirs, assigns, legal representatives, members of his family and all persons inducted by him into the demised land.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Eviction of outgoing lessee from land or building</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. If on the expiry, whether before or after the commencement of this Ordinance, of the period of a lease in respect of any land or building of which the Government or a Local Authority is the lessor or on the determination of such lease on the ground of breach of any covenant or on the determination of such lease according to the terms and conditions of the lease or otherwise, the lessee refused or failed, or refuses or fails, to vacate that land or building and put the lessor into possession of the same, then, notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force or in any contract, it shall be lawful for the Deputy Commissioner, on his own motion or on the complaint of or upon information received from anybody or a Local Authority, at any time after the expiry or determination of lease, to re-enter upon the demised land or building and recover khas possession thereof by evicting the lessee and by demolishing and removing structures, if any, erected or built thereon by the lessee:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Deputy Commissioner shall, before demolishing and removing any structures under this section, issue, in the prescribed manner, a notice on the lessee calling upon him to remove such structures within a period of thirty days from the date of service of the notice.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Determination of lease and recovery of building in certain cases</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force or any contract, where the lessee of a building or part of a building 4[ is a person in the service of the Republic] or of a Local Authority, the lease in respect of such</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">building or part shall, in addition to the modes mentioned in section 111 of the Transfer of Property Act, 1882, terminate-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        on the suspension, discharge, removal, dismissal, resignation, retirement or death of such servant or on his transfer from the station in which he is employed to any other station; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        on the transfer of the lessee's interest by assignment, mortgage, sub-lease or in any other manner.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) On the determination of a lease in respect of a building or part of a building in the manner stated in sub-section (1) or in any of the modes mentioned in section 111 of the Transfer of Property Act, 1882, the lessee or the person claiming through him shall, notwithstanding anything contained elsewhere in the said Act or in any other law for the time being in force or in any contract, forthwith put the lessor into possession of such building or part, failing which it shall be lawful for the Deputy Commissioner to re-enter and recover khas possession of the same by evicting the lessee or the person claiming through him:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Deputy Commissioner shall, before re-entering such building or part of a building, issue, in the prescribed manner, a notice on such lessee or person calling upon him to vacate the same within a period of thirty days from the date of service of the notice.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Eviction of unauthorised occupant</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) If the Deputy Commissioner, on his own motion or on the complaint of or upon information received from anybody or a Local Authority, is satisfied after making such inquiry as he thinks fit, that a person is an unauthorised occupant, he may issue, in the prescribed manner, a notice directing such person to vacate the land, building or part thereof in his occupation within a period of thirty days from the date of service of the notice 5[ :</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Deputy Commissioner may, where he is satisfied that thirty days' notice will not be in public interest, reduce the period of such notice to not less than seven days.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) If the person, against whom an order under sub-section (1) has been made, refuses or fails to vacate the land, building or part thereof in his occupation within the time fixed, then, notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force, it shall be lawful for the Deputy Commissioner to enter upon such land, building or part thereof and recover khas possession of the same by evicting such person and by demolishing and removing structures, if any, erected or built by that person.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Mode of recovery of possession</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. For the purpose of recovering khas possession of any land, building or part thereof under the provisions of section 3 or section 4 or section 5, the Deputy Commissioner may use or cause to be used such force as may be necessary.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalties</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained elsewhere in this Ordinance or in any other law for the time being in force, if a Deputy Commissioner, an Additional Deputy Commissioner, a Joint Deputy Commissioner or a 6[ Upazilla Nirbahi Officer], on his own motion or on the complaint of or upon an information received from anybody, is satisfied after making such inquiry as he may think fit, that a person is an unauthorised occupant of any land or building or part thereof, he may give or cause to be given an information to that effect to the Police Station having jurisdiction and thereupon it would be an offence which shall be punishable with imprisonment of either description for a term not exceeding two years or with fine which may extend to rupees one thousand or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An offence punishable under sub-section (1) shall be a cognizable and non-bailable offence to be tried in accordance with the warrant procedure as laid down in the Code of Criminal Procedure.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Forfeiture</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. All structures and other properties remaining on the land, building or part thereof, after expiry of the period specified in the notice under section 3 or section 4 or section 5, shall be forfeited to the Government or the Local Authority, as the case may be.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Compensation for unauthorised occupation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. (1) For unauthorised occupation of any land, building or part thereof or for any damage caused thereto, the unauthorised occupant shall be liable to pay to the Government or to the Local Authority, as the case may be, such compensation as may be assessed by the Deputy Commissioner in accordance with the rules to be made in this behalf by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) As soon as an assessment has been made under sub-section (1), the Deputy Commissioner shall serve on the assessee, in the prescribed manner, a notice of such assessment, directing him to pay the amount so assessed within the period of thirty days from the date of service of the notice.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Any amount due under sub-section (2) or if the rent payable for lease in respect of any land, building or part of any building has been in arrear, such amount or rent shall be recoverable as public demand under the provisions of 7[ * * *] Public Demands Recovery Act, 1913.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appeal</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. Any person aggrieved by an order made under section 3 or section 4 or section 5 or section 9 may prefer an appeal to the 8[ Commissioner of the Division] within thirty days of the service of notice and the decision of the 9[ Commissioner] on such an appeal shall be final.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Bar to jurisdiction of civil Court</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. No civil Court shall pass an order in any suit or proceeding granting a temporary or ad interim injunction restraining the Deputy Commissioner from taking possession of any land, building or part thereof under this Ordinance nor shall call in question any assessment of compensation made under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Public servant</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. Any person authorised to exercise any power or discharge any duty under this Ordinance shall be deemed to be a public servant under section 21 of the 10[ * * *] Penal Code.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Indemnity</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. (1) No suit or legal proceeding shall lie against the Government or a Local Authority in respect of anything which is, in good faith, done or intended to be done under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No suit, prosecution or legal proceeding shall lie against any person in respect of anything which is, in good faith, done or intended to be done under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15. [Repeal and savings.- Omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the words “Bangladesh” and “Government” were substituted for the words “East Pakistan” and “Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words, brackets, figures and comma “clause (28) of section 3 of the General Clauses Act, 1897 (X of 1897)” were substituted for the words, brackets, figures and comma “clause (23) of section 3 of the Bengal General Clauses Act, 1899 (Bengal Act I of 1899)” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The words “is a person in the service of the Republic” were substituted for the words “is a servant of Government in Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The colon (:) was substituted for the full-stop (.) and the proviso was added thereafter by Article 2 of the Bangladesh Government and Local Authority Lands and Buildings (Recovery of Possession) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 85 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The words “Upazilla Nirbahi Officer” were substituted for the words “Sub-divisional Officer” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The word “Bengal” was omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The words “Commissioner of the Division” were substituted for the word “Government” by the Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Amending) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. IX of 1976)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 The word “Commissioner” was substituted for the word “Government” by the Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Amending) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. IX of 1976)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
351	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE IMPORT OF GOODS (PRICE EQUALISATION SURCHARGE) ACT, 1967 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE IMPORT OF GOODS (PRICE EQUALISATION SURCHARGE) ACT, 1967 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ACT NO. III OF 1967).[3rd June, 1967]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Act to levy an additional duty for equalisation of prices of certain imported goods.     1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to levy an additional duty for equalisation of prices of certain goods imported at different prices under different conditions and from different countries and to provide for matters ancillary thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Act may be called the Import of Goods (Price Equalisation Surcharge) Act, 1967.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) “highest rate”, in relation to any specified goods imported in any shipping period, means the highest rate of landed cost declared in relation to such goods under sub-section (1) of section 4;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) “landed cost”, in relation to any specified goods, means the aggregate of the c.i.f. value, duties, taxes, fees and other charges payable on or for the import of such goods into Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “price equalisation surcharge” means the additional duty levied under section 3;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) “shipping period” means a period beginning on the first day of January and ending on the thirtieth day of June, or a period beginning on the first day of July and ending on thirty-first day of December, each year or such other period as the Government may, from time to time, by notification in the official Gazette, declare to be a shipping period for the purposes of this Act; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        “specified goods” means such of the goods specified in the Schedule as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare to be the goods which shall be subject to the levy of the price equalisation surcharge.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Levy of price equalisation surcharge</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. There shall be levied on the specified goods imported in any shipping period into Bangladesh after the 22nd day of April, 1966, or, if the Government, in respect of any specified goods by order so directs, after such later date as may be specified therein, whose rate of landed cost is lower than the highest rate, an additional duty as price equalisation surcharge at the rate by which the rate of the landed cost of such goods falls short of the highest rate.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to authorise repayment of surcharge</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2[ 3A. Subject to such conditions, limitations or restrictions as it may think fit to impose, the Government may, in such general cases as it may prescribe by rules or in particular cases by special order, authorise the repayment in whole or in part of the price equalisation surcharge paid on the importation of any goods of such classes or descriptions as may be prescribed in the rules or specified in the special order, as the case may be.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Determination of highest landed cost</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) The Government shall determine and, by notification in the official Gazette, declare, in relation to every specified goods imported in any shipping period, the highest rate of landed cost of such goods.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) For the purpose of determining the highest rate, every importer of specified goods shall furnish at such time such papers, documents or information relating to the import of such goods, as the Government may direct.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Whoever fails or neglects to comply with any direction under sub-section (2) shall be deemed to have contravened the provisions of the Imports and Exports (Control) Act, 1950, and shall be punishable under section 5 of that Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Procedure for collection of price equalisation surcharge</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. Subject to any rules made under this Act, the price equalisation surcharge shall be collected in the same manner as an import duty payable under the Tariff Act, 1934 is collected and the provisions of the 3[ Customs Act, 1969 (IV of 1969)] shall, so far as may be, apply to the levy, collection and repayment of such surcharge.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing power, such rules may provide for-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        the assessment, collection and repayment of the price equalisation surcharge;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the delivery of goods on the giving of security for payment of such surcharge or on any other conditions;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the manner of payment and repayment of such surcharge; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) such other matters as may be necessary for carrying out the purposes of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to amend Schedule</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4[ 6A. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make any addition to or omission from the list of goods specified in the Schedule.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[Repealed]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. [Validation.- Repealed by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Act, the words “Bangladesh” and “Government” were substituted for the words “Pakistan” and “Central Government” respectively by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 Section 3A was inserted by section 12 of the Finance Act, 1968 (Act No. XI of 1968)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words, comma, figures and brackets “Customs Act, 1969 (IV of 1969)” were substituted for the words, comma, figures and brackets “Sea Customs Act, 1878 (VIII of 1878)” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 Section 6A was inserted by section 12 of the Finance Act, 1968 (Act No. XI of 1968)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
352	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE MONOPOLIES AND RESTRICTIVE TRADE PRACTICES (CONTROL AND PREVENTION) ORDINANCE, 1970 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE MONOPOLIES AND RESTRICTIVE TRADE PRACTICES (CONTROL AND PREVENTION) ORDINANCE, 1970 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ORDINANCE NO. V OF 1970).[26th February, 1970]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to provide for measures against undue concentration of economic power, growth of unreasonable monopoly power and unreasonably restrictive trade practices.        1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS the undue concentration of economic power, growth of unreasonable monopoly power and unreasonably restrictive trade practices are injurious to the economic wellbeing, growth and development of Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS it is expedient to provide for measures against such concentration, growth and practices and for matters connected therewith or incidental thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS the national interest of Pakistan in relation to the economic and financial stability of Pakistan requires Central legislation in the matter;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the 25th day of March, 1969, read with the Provisional Constitution Order, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the President is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>CHAPTER I</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>PRELIMINARY</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the Monopolies and Restrictive Trade Practices (Control and Prevention) Ordinance, 1970.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force on such date as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. (1) In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “agreement” includes any arrangement or understanding whether or not in writing and whether or not it is or is intended to be legally enforceable;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “associated undertakings” means any two or more undertakings interconnected with each other in the following manner, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         if a person who is the owner or a partner, officer or director of an undertaking or who directly or indirectly holds or controls shares carrying not less than twenty per cent of the voting power in such undertaking, is also the owner or a partner, officer or director of another undertaking or, directly or indirectly, holds or controls shares carrying not less than twenty per cent of the voting power in that undertaking;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        if the undertakings are under common management or common control or one is the subsidiary of another;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “Authority” means the Monopoly Control Authority constituted under section 8;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        “control”, in relation to an undertaking, means the power to exercise a controlling influence over the management or the policies of the undertaking, and, in relation to shares, means the power to exercise a controlling influence over the voting power attached to such shares;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        “individual” includes a Hindu undivided family;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         “market”, in relation to any goods or services, means the geographic region in which competition in the production or sale of such goods or the provision of such services takes place;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        “monopoly power” means the ability of one or more sellers in a market to set non-competitive prices or restrict output without losing a substantial share of the market or to exclude others from any part of that market;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h) “price”, in relation to the sale of any goods or to the provision of any services, includes every valuable consideration, whether direct or indirect, which in effect relates to the sale of any goods or the provision of any services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) “retailer”, in relation to the sale of any goods, means a person who sells the goods to any other person otherwise than for re-sale;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(j)         “service” means provision of board, lodging, transport, entertainment or amusement, or of facilities in connection with the supply of electrical or other energy, purveying of news, banking, insurance or investment;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(k)        “trade” means any business, industry, profession or occupation relating to the production, supply or distribution of goods or the control of production, supply or distribution of goods, or to the provision or control of any service;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(l)         “trade practice” means any act or practice relating to the carrying on of any trade or business;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(m)       “undertaking” means any concern, institution, establishment or enterprise engaged in the production, supply or distribution of goods, or in the provision or control of any service;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(n)        “unreasonably restrictive trade practice” means a trade practice which has or may have the effect of unreasonably preventing, restraining or otherwise lessening competition in any manner;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(o)        “value of assets”, in relation to an undertaking, means the value of assets of the undertaking at cost less depreciation at the normal rates at which depreciation is calculated for purpose of assessment of income-tax;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(p)        “wholesaler”, in relation to the sale of any goods, means a person who purchases goods and sells them to any other person for re-sale; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(q)        words and expressions used but not defined in this Ordinance and defined in the 2[ Companies Act, 1994 (Act No. XVIII of 1994)], have the meanings respectively assigned to them in that Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) For the purposes of this Ordinance an individual shall be deemed to own, hold or control a thing if it is owned, held or controlled by the individual or his spouse, or by a brother or sister of the individual, or by any of the lineal ascendants or descendants of the individual.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER II</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">UNDUE CONCENTRATION OF ECONOMIC POWER, ETC., PROHIBITED</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Undue concentration of economic power, etc, prohibited</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. There shall be no undue concentration of economic power, unreasonable monopoly power or unreasonably restrictive trade practices.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Circumstances constituting undue concentration of economic power</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. Undue concentration of economic power shall be deemed to have been brought about, maintained or continued if-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        there is established, run or continued an undertaking the total value of whose assets is not less than one crore of Taka, or such other amount as the Authority may by rule prescribe, and which is-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) not owned by a public company, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        is owned by a public company in which any individual holds or controls shares carrying not less than fifty per cent, or such other percentage as the Authority may by rule prescribe, of the voting power in the undertaking;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        there are any dealings between associated undertakings which have or are likely to have the effect of unfairly benefiting the owners or share-holders of one such undertaking to the prejudice of the owners or share-holders of any other of its associated undertakings.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Circumstances constituting unreasonable monopoly power</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) Unreasonable monopoly power shall be deemed to have been brought about, maintained and continued if-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        there has been created or maintained any such relationship between two or more undertakings as makes them associated undertakings where they are competitors in the same market and together produce, supply, distribute or provide not less than twenty per cent of the total goods or services in such market;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        there has been any acquisition by one person or undertaking of the stock or assets of any other person or undertaking, or any merger of undertakings, where the effect of the acquisition or merger is likely to create monopoly power or to substantially lessen competition in any market, including any acquisition which creates any such relationship as is referred to in clause (a);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        any loan is granted by a bank or insurance company to any of the associated undertakings of amounts greater or on terms more favourable than for loans made available to other undertakings in comparable situations, or any loan is granted by a bank or insurance company to a person or undertaking not associated with it on the condition or understanding that the borrower or any of its associated undertakings will make any loan to a person or undertaking associated with the lender.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No such relationship, acquisition, merger or loan as is referred to in sub-section (1) shall be deemed to have the effect of bringing about, maintaining or continuing unreasonable monopoly power if it is shown-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        that it contributes substantially to the efficiency of the production or distribution of goods or of the provision of services or to the promotion of technical progress or export of goods;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        that such efficiency or promotion could not reasonably have been achieved by means less restrictive of competition; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        that the benefits of such efficiency or promotion clearly outweigh the adverse effect of the absence or lessening of competition.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Unreasonably restrictive trade practices</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) Unreasonably restrictive trade practices shall be deemed to have been resorted to or continued if there is any agreement-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        between actual or potential competitors for the purpose or having the effect of-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         fixing the purchase or selling prices or imposing any other restrictive trading conditions with regard to the sale or distribution of any goods or the provision of any services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        dividing or sharing of markets for any goods or services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       limiting the quantity or the means of production, distribution or sale regard to any goods or the manner or means of providing any services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv)       limiting technical development or investment with regard to the production, distribution or sale of any goods or the provision of services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(v)        excluding by means of boycott any other person or undertaking from the production, distribution or sale of any goods or the provision of any services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        between a supplier and a dealer of goods fixing minimum resale prices, including-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         an agreement with a condition for the sale of goods by a supplier to a dealer which purports to establish or provide for the minimum prices to be charged on the resale of the goods in Bangladesh; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        an agreement which requires as a condition of supplying goods to a dealer to the making of any such agreement;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        which subjects the making of any agreement to the acceptance by suppliers or buyers of additional goods or services which are not, by their nature or by the custom of the trade, related to the subject matter of such agreement.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No such agreement as is referred to in sub-section (1) shall be deemed to constitute an unreasonably restrictive trade practice if it is shown-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        that it contributes substantially to the efficiency of the production or distribution of goods or of the provision of</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">services or to the promotion of technical progress or export of goods;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        that such efficiency or promotion could not reasonably have been achieved by means less restrictive of competition; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        that the benefits from such efficiency or promotion clearly outweigh the adverse effect of the absence or lessening of competition.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Other circumstances constituting concentration of economic power, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. (1) Without prejudice to the provisions of sections 4, 5 and 6, the Authority may by General Order prescribe the circumstances in which and the conditions under which undue concentration of economic power or unreasonable monopoly power shall be deemed to exist and the practices which shall be deemed to be unreasonably restrictive trade practices.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Where the Authority is of opinion that the making of a General Order under sub-section (1) may be in the public interest, it shall conduct an inquiry affording the persons or undertakings likely to be affected by such Order such opportunity of being heard and of placing before it relevant facts and material as it may deem fit.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Before making any General Order under sub-section (1), the Authority shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        publish in the official Gazette and in such other manner as in its opinion will bring it to the notice of all persons and undertakings likely to be affected thereby a draft of the proposed General Order together with a notice inviting suggestions or objections to be submitted before a date specified therein;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        consider any objection or suggestion which may be received by it from any person or undertaking with respect to the draft; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        where it deems appropriate, afford an opportunity to any such person or undertaking of being heard and of placing before it facts and material in support of the objection or suggestion.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER III</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">MONOPOLY CONTROL AUTHORITY</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Constitution of Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. (1) For the purposes of this Ordinance, the Government shall, by notification in the official Gazette, constitute a Monopoly Control Authority consisting of not less than three members appointed by it one of whom shall be appointed to be the Chairman.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No person shall be appointed as, or continue to be, a member of the Authority if he has or acquires any such financial or other interest as is likely to affect prejudicially his functions as such member.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) No member of the Authority shall assume his office until he has made such declaration affirming secrecy and fidelity as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) A member of the Authority shall hold office for a period of five years unless he earlier resigns or otherwise ceases to hold office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) A casual vacancy in the office of a member caused by death, resignation or otherwise shall be filled for the remainder of the term of such member by the appointment of another person.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) No act or proceeding of the Authority shall be invalid by reason only of the existence of any vacancy among its members or any defect in its constitution.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appointment of officers by the Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. The Authority may appoint such officers and servants on such terms and conditions as it may determine.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER IV</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">FUNCTIONS AND POWERS OF THE AUTHORITY</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Functions of the Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. The functions of the Authority shall be-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        to register undertakings, individuals and agreements;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        to conduct enquiries into the general economic conditions of the country with particular reference to the concentration of economic power and the existence or growth of monopoly power and restrictive trade practices;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) to conduct such enquiry into the affairs of any undertaking or individual as may be necessary for the purposes of this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) to give advice to persons or undertakings asking for the same as to whether any actions proposed to be taken by such person or undertaking are consistent with the provisions of this Ordinance, or any rules or orders made thereunder;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) to make recommendations to the Government or a Provincial Government or to the appropriate authority or officer of such Government for suitable Governmental actions to prevent or eliminate undue concentration of economic power, unreasonable monopoly power or unreasonably restrictive trade practices; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) to make such orders and to do all such things as are necessary for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Proceedings in case of contravention of section 3</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. (1) Where the Authority is satisfied that there has been or is likely to be a contravention of the provisions of section 3 and that action is necessary in the public interest, it may make one or more of such orders specified in section 12 as it may deem appropriate.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Before making an order under sub-section (1), the Authority shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        give notice of its intention to make such order stating the reasons therefore to such persons or undertakings as may appear to it to be concerned in the contravention to show cause on or before a date specified therein as to why such order shall not be made; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        give the persons or undertakings an opportunity of being heard and of placing before it facts and material in support of their contention.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) An order made under sub-section (1) shall have effect notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force or in any contract or memorandum or articles of association.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Orders of the Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. (1) An order of the Authority under section 11 may,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        in the case of undue concentration of economic power-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         require the firms or companies concerned, not being public limited companies, to be converted, within such time and in such manner as may be specified in the order, into public limited companies;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        require the controlling shareholders of the public limited companies concerned to offer such part of the stocks and shares held by them within such time and in such manner as may be specified in the order to the general public, including 3[ * * *] an investment institution established or controlled by Government;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       prescribe the circumstances in which and the conditions on which the associated undertakings concerned may deal with each other;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        in the case of unreasonable monopoly power,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) require the person or undertaking concerned to divest himself or itself of the ownership of any stock or shares or other beneficial interest in any undertaking or of any assets within such time and under such conditions as may be specified in the order;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        require the person concerned to divest himself of any position held by him as an officer, director or partner in any undertaking within such time and under such conditions as may be specified in the order;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       require the person or undertaking concerned to divest himself or itself of the management or control of any undertaking within such time and under such conditions as may be specified in the order;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv)       prohibit the person or undertaking concerned from acquiring the stock or assets of, or the undertaking from merging with, any other undertaking;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(v)        limit the total loans which may be made by any bank or insurance company to any single individual or undertaking, or to any undertaking associated with such bank or insurance company;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vi)       limit the investments of any undertaking engaged in the banking, investment or insurance business;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vii)      require the person or undertaking concerned to take such actions specified in the order as may be necessary to restore competitive prices and eliminate restrictions on output or entry of competitors in the market;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) in the case of unreasonably restrictive trade practices,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         require the person or undertaking concerned to discontinue or not to repeat any restrictive trade practice and to terminate or modify any agreement relating thereto in such manner as may be specified in the order;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        require the person or undertaking concerned to take such actions specified in the order as may be necessary to restore competition in the production, distribution or sale of any goods or provision of any services.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An order referred to in sub-clause (ii) of clause (a) of sub-section (1) or sub-clause (i) of clause (b) of that sub-section shall not be so made as to require the offer of the stocks or shares at a price below their face value or at a price below the aggregate of such value and fifty per cent of the difference between such value and the net worth of the stocks or shares as may be determined in accordance with the rules made in this behalf, which ever is greater.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Where any stocks or shares have been offered in pursuance of an order referred to in sub-section (2), no fresh order of such nature shall be made in respect of the same person or undertaking within a period of three years from the date of such order whether or not the stocks or shares offered have actually been subscribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to issue interim order</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. (1) Where, during the course of any proceeding under section 11, the Authority is of opinion that issue of a final order in the proceeding is likely to take time and that, in the situation that exists or is likely to emerge, an interim order is necessary in the public interest, it may, after giving the persons or undertakings concerned an opportunity of being heard, by order, direct such persons or undertakings to do or refrain from doing or continuing to do any act or thing specified in the order.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An order under sub-section (1) may, at any time, be modified or cancelled by the Authority and, unless so cancelled, shall remain in force for such period as may be specified therein but not beyond the date of the final order made under section 11.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Special enquiry</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. (1) The Authority may, on its own, and shall upon a reference made to it by the Government, conduct special enquiries into any matter relevant to the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2)Where the Authority receives from not less than twenty five persons a complaint in writing of such facts as constitute a contravention of the provisions of section 3, it shall, unless it is of opinion that the application is frivolous or vexatious or based on insufficient facts, conduct a special enquiry into the matter to which the complaint relates.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) If upon the conclusion of a special inquiry under sub-section (1) or sub-section (2), the Authority is of opinion that the findings are such that it is necessary in the public interest so to do, it shall initiate proceedings under section 11.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Powers of the Authority in relation to a proceeding or enquiry</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15. (1) The Authority shall, for the purposes of a proceeding or enquiry under this Ordinance, have the same powers as are vested in a civi1 Court under the Code of Civil Procedure, 1908, while trying a suit, in respect of the following matters, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        the summoning and enforcing the attendance of any witness and examining him on oath;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        the discovery and production of any document or other material object producible as evidence;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the reception of evidence on affidavits;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        the requisitioning of any public record from any Court or office;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        the issuing of commissions for the examination of witnesses and documents.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Any proceeding before the Authority shall be deemed to be a judicial proceeding within the meaning of sections 193 and 228 of the 4[ * * *] Penal Code, and the Authority shall be deemed to be a civil Court for the purposes of section 195 and Chapter XXXV of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Authority may, for the purposes of a proceeding or enquiry under this Ordinance, require any person-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        to produce before, and to allow to be examined and kept by, an officer of the Authority specified in this behalf, any books, accounts, or other documents in the custody or under the control of the person so required, being documents relating to any matter the examination of which may be necessary for the purposes of this Ordinance; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        to furnish to an officer so specified such information in his possession relating to any matter as may be necessary for the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER V</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">REGISTRATION</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Registration</p><p style="text-align: justify;">16. (1) In order that information relevant to the performance of its functions under this Ordinance is available to the Authority, the following undertakings, individuals and agreements shall be registered with the Authority in such manner as may be prescribed by rules, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) An undertaking which, during the next preceding calendar year produced, distributed, sold or provided not less than one-third of the total production or supply of any goods or services 5[ * * *] .</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) Associated undertakings engaged in the same line of business, which during the next preceding calendar year produced, distributed, sold or provided not less than twenty per cent of the total production or supply of any goods or services 6[ * * *].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        An undertaking which during the next preceding calendar year, by itself or together with its associated undertaking, both produced and distributed by wholesale or by retail or by both not less than twenty per cent of the total production and supply of any goods 7[ * * *].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) An undertaking which is not owned by a public company and the total value of the assets of which is not less than one crore of Taka.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) An undertaking which, by agreement or otherwise, establishes minimum resale prices for retailers or wholesalers with regard to goods which it produces or distributes.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) An undertaking which, by itself or together with its associated undertaking, is the sole distributor or supplier 8[ * * *] for more than one undertakings of any goods or services.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        A bank, investment company or insurance company which, in relation to any other undertaking, is an associated undertaking.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h)        An individual who holds or controls, whether directly or indirectly, shares carrying not less than fifty per cent of the voting power in an undertaking owned by a public company the total value of the assets of which is not less than one crore of Taka.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) An agreement for any such acquisition or merger as is referred to in clause (b) of sub-section (1) of section 5.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(j) An agreement of the nature referred to in sub-section (1) of section 6.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(k) An agreement for the distribution or sale of any goods which, directly or indirectly,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         limits the areas in which, or the persons to whom, the product may be re-sold;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        prohibits or restricts the distribution or sale of other goods by the distributor;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       limits the persons through whom the distributor may distribute or sell such goods.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(l) Any license of patents or technology which limits the freedom of the licensee to use such patents or technology in the manufacture of any goods or to sell the goods produced under such license at such prices, in such areas, to such persons and for such uses as the licensee may choose, or which limits the freedom of the licensor to grant additional licenses to such persons and on such terms as he may choose.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(m)       Such other persons, undertakings, agreements or franchise as the Authority may by rule prescribe.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Explanation.- For the purposes of clauses (a),(b) and (c), the percentage of any goods produced, distributed or sold or of any services provided shall be computed on the basis of the monthly statistical bulletin of the 9[ Government] or on such other basis as the Authority may by rule prescribe.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An application for registration under sub-section (1) shall be made in the form of a memorandum which shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        in the case of an undertaking, set out the value of its assets, the volume of each of the goods or services sold or provided by it, and the full particulars of the facts by reason of which it is subject to registration;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        in the case of an individual, set out a statement of the extent and nature of his control over an undertaking or its shares, by reason of which he is subject to registration;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        in the case of an agreement, set out the names and addresses of the persons who are parties to the agreement and be accompanied by a true copy of the agreement or, if the agreement is not in writing, by the full particulars of the agreement.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) An application for
