registration shall be made-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) in the case of an undertaking, by the person who is for the time being responsible for the conduct of the affairs of the undertaking;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        in the case of an individual, by such individual; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) in the case of an agreement, by all the parties thereto.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Explanation.- The provisions of this sub-section shall be deemed to have been complied with if the application is made-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        in the case of an undertaking, by the person for the time being responsible for the conduct of the affairs of any one of its associated undertakings;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        in the case of an individual other than a Hindu undivided family, by any one of his relations referred to in sub-section (2) of section 2;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        in the case of a Hindu undivided family, by any member of the family; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        in the case of an agreement, by any one of the parties thereto.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) If at any time there is any variation in the relevant facts relating to an undertaking, individual or agreement with reference to which an application for registration was made or registration was effected, particulars of such variation shall, within thirty days of the variation, be reported to the Authority by the person referred to in sub-section (3).</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Registers to be kept</p><p style="text-align: justify;">17. (1) The Authority shall keep and maintain in such form as may be prescribed by rules separate registers for the registration of undertakings, individuals and agreements subject to registration under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Authority shall register an undertaking, individual or agreement by entering in the register such particulars relating thereto as may be prescribed by rules.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Authority shall enter in the register any variation in the facts relating to an undertaking, individual or agreement reported to it.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) A register shall be open to public inspection at such time and on payment of such fees as may be prescribed by rules, except that the Authority may, upon application by the person or undertaking concerned, provide for the confidential treatment of trade secrets.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Cancellation of registration</p><p style="text-align: justify;">18. Where an undertaking, individual or agreement registered under section 16 has, by reason of a change in the facts, with reference to which the registration was effected, ceased to be subject to registration under this Ordinance and the fact is reported to the Authority by the person referred to in sub-section (3) of section 16, the Authority shall, if it is satisfied upon such inquiry as it may think fit that the undertaking, individual or agreement has so ceased, cancel the registration.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">CHAPTER VI</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">PENALTIES AND APPEALS</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalty</p><p style="text-align: justify;">19. (1) The Authority may, by order, direct any person or undertaking to pay to the Government by way of penalty such sum not exceeding one lakh of Taka as may be specified in the order if, after giving the person or undertaking concerned an opportunity of being heard, it determines that such person or undertaking-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        has failed to comply with any order of the Authority made under this Ordinance, or has wilfully failed to register as required by the provisions of this Ordinance, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        has furnished any information or made any statement to the Authority which he knows or has reason to believe to be false in any material particular.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) If any such failure as is referred to in clause (a) of that sub-section is a continuing one, the Authority may in the manner provided for in sub-section (1) also direct that the person or undertaking guilty of such failure shall pay by way of penalty to the Government a further sum which may extend to ten thousand Taka for every day after the first.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) A penalty imposed under sub-section (1) or sub-section (2) shall be recoverable as an arrear of land revenue.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appeal to the 10[ High Court Division]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">20. Any person aggrieved by an order of the Authority under section 11 or section 19 may, within sixty days of the receipt of such order, appeal against it to the 11[ High Court Division] on any of the following grounds, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        that the order is contrary to law or to some usage having the force of law;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) that the order has failed to determine some material issue of law or usage having the force of law;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) that there has been a substantial error or defect in following the procedure provided in this Ordinance which may possibly have produced error or defect in the order upon the merits.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to call for information relating to undertakings</p><p style="text-align: justify;">21. Notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force, the Authority may, by general or special order, call upon any person for the time being responsible for the conduct of the affairs of an undertaking to furnish periodically or as and when required any information concerning the activities of the undertaking, including information relating to its organisation, business, trade practices, management and connection with any other undertaking, which the Authority may consider necessary or useful for the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Compensation not payable</p><p style="text-align: justify;">22. No person shall be entitled to or be paid any compensation or damages for any loss or injury suffered by him on account of the termination of any agreement or employment or the divestment of any share or property in pursuance of any order made under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Indemnity</p><p style="text-align: justify;">23. No suit, prosecution or other legal proceeding shall lie against the Authority or any officer or servant of the Authority for anything in good faith done or intended to be done under this Ordinance or any rule or order made thereunder.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">24. The Authority may make and publish rules regarding procedures, fees and all other matters for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Ordinance not to apply to certain undertakings</p><p style="text-align: justify;">25. This Ordinance shall not, unless the Government by notification in the official Gazette otherwise directs, apply-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) to an undertaking which is owned by the 12[ Government], or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        to an undertaking which is owned by a body corporate established by the Government by law or whose Chief Executive is appointed by or with the approval of the 13[ Government], or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) to anything done by any person or undertaking in pursuance of any order of the 14[ Government], or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) to anything done by a trade union or its members for carrying out its purposes.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the words “Bangladesh”, “Government” and “Taka” were substituted for the words “Pakistan”, “Central Government” and “rupees” respectively by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words, comma, figures and brackets “Companies Act, 1994 (Act No. XVIII of 1994)” were substituted for the words, comma, figures and brackets “Companies Act, 1913 (VII of 1913)” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words “the National Investment Trust and” were omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “in any Province” were omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The words “in any Province” were omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The words “in any Province” were omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The words “in any Province” were omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Statistical Office of the Central Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10 The words, comma, figures and brackets “Companies Act, 1994 (Act No. XVIII of 1994)” were substituted for the words, comma, figures and brackets “Companies Act, 1913 (VII of 1913)” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">11 The words “High Court Division” were substituted for the words “High Court” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">12 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Government or a Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">13 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Government or by a Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">14 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Government or a Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
353	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">  THE NATIONAL SERVICE ORDINANCE, 1970 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE NATIONAL SERVICE ORDINANCE, 1970 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ORDINANCE NO. XXII OF 1970).[7th November, 1970]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to introduce compulsory national service in Bangladesh.    1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to introduce compulsory national service in Bangladesh and to provide for matters ancillary thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the 25th day of March, 1969, read with the Provisional Constitution Order, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the President is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance :-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent, application and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 2[ * * *] National Service Ordinance, 1970.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh and applies to all citizens of Bangladesh wherever they may be.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force on such day as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint in this behalf.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “emoluments”, in relation to a person, includes the pay, allowances, gratuity, fees, commissions, perquisites and profits which such person is entitled to receive from his employer for his services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “employer” means any person or body of persons, whether incorporated or not, who or which employs another person for hire or reward, either directly or through a contractor, whether the terms of employment be express or implied and includes, in the case of an establishment, the person responsible for the management, supervision and control of the establishment;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “essential service” means any service which the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare to be essential for securing the defence or the security of Bangladesh or of any part thereof or for the maintenance of supplies and services essential to the life of the community;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        “establishment” means any office, firm, industrial unit, undertaking, shop or premises in which persons are employed for the purpose of carrying on any manufacturing process, business, trade or service;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        “matriculate” means a person who has passed the Matriculation Examination or Secondary School Leaving Certificate Examination, or any other equivalent examination, of a board or other authority set up by Government or by or under any law and includes a person who has passed such other examination as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare to be equivalent of such examination;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) “national service” means the service required to be rendered under sub-section (4) of section 5; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        “prescribed” means prescribed by rules made under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">National service liability, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) Subject to the provisions of this Ordinance, every male citizen of Bangladesh who has attained the age of eighteen years and has not attained the age of twenty years and possesses educational qualifications not below that of a matriculate shall be liable to render national service.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Every male citizen of Bangladesh who, at the commencement of this Ordinance, has attained the age of eighteen years and has not attained the age of twenty years and possesses educational qualifications not below that of a matriculate shall, not later than one month from such commencement, offer himself for national service in such manner and to such authority as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Every male citizen of Bangladesh who, at any time after the commencement of this Ordinance,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        being a matriculate, attains the age of eighteen years, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) having attained the age of eighteen years, becomes a matriculate,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">shall, not later than one month from the date on which he attains the age of eighteen years or, as the case may be, becomes a matriculate, offer himself for national service in such manner and to such authority as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Nothing in sub-section (1), sub-section (2) or sub-section (3) shall apply to persons-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        who are members of any of the Defence Services or civilian armed forces of, or any police force in, Bangladesh or are employed in any of the ordnance factories in Bangladesh; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        who, being engaged in any essential service or being students of any medical, engineering or veterinary institution, are declared by the Government, by notification in the official Gazette, to be exempt from the liability to render national service.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Deferment of liability to render national service</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) The liability to render national service of any person who is a student of any institution may, on an application made in this behalf to the prescribed authority, be deferred for such period as the authority may deem fit having regard to the duration of the course of studies taken up by such person.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Where the liability of any person to render national service has been deferred for any period under sub-section (1), the age up to which he is liable to be called up for such service shall be deemed to be extended by that period.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Selection and enrolment, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) An officer or authority prescribed in this behalf may, by a notice in writing, require any person liable to render national service to report in person to such authority and at such time and place as may be specified in the notice and the person to whom a notice has been issued shall report accordingly.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A person who has reported in pursuance of a notice under sub-section (1) shall be selected for national service unless-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        his liability to render national service has for the time being been deferred under section 4; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        he is exempted after medical examination from the requirement of rendering national service; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        he is exempted from the requirement of rendering national service in accordance with rules made under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) A person selected under sub-section (2) shall report to such authority and at such time and place as may be specified by the authority by whom he is so selected for the purpose of being enrolled in the Bangladesh Army, the Bangladesh Navy or, as the case may be, the Bangladesh Air Force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) A person who has reported under sub-section (3) shall, subject to the provisions of this Ordinance and the rules made thereunder, render national service for a period of one year in the Bangladesh Army, the Bangladesh Navy or, as the case may be, the Bangladesh Air Force in which he shall be enrolled for that period.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) Save as otherwise provided in the rules made under this Ordinance, a person, while he is rendering national service, shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) be subject to the service law of the Defence Service in which he is enrolled for such service; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) receive such honorarium per month as may be prescribed and be entitled to such other facilities and privileges, other than salary, as are admissible to a person enrolled in the Bangladesh Army, the Bangladesh Navy or, as the case may be, the Bangladesh Air Force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">National Service Reserve</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. A person who has completed national service shall be placed on the National Service Reserve created for the purposes of this Ordinance and shall, until he has attained the age of thirty-five years, be liable to be called up -</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        for refresher training every year; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        for service from time to time in the Defence Service in which he rendered national service.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Refresher training</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. (1) A person in the National Service Reserve shall, when called up for training under clause (a) of section 6 by a notice in writing by the officer or authority prescribed in this behalf, report in person to such authority and at such time and place as may be specified in the notice and shall receive in the Defence Service in which he rendered national service the prescribed training for the prescribed period which shall not be less than fifteen days or more than thirty days.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Save as otherwise provided in this Ordinance or the rules made thereunder, a person, while he is undergoing training in a Defence Service under sub-section (1), shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        be subject to the 3[ * * *] Army Act, 1952, the 4[ * * *] Navy Ordinance, 1961, or, as the case may be, the 5[ * * *] Air Force Act, 1953; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) receive such honorarium as may be prescribed and be entitled to such other facilities and privileges, other than salary, as are admissible to a person enrolled in the Defence Service in which he is undergoing training.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Service in Defence Services</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. (1) A person in the National Service Reserve shall, when called up for service in a Defence Service under clause (b) of section 6 by a notice in writing by the officer or authority prescribed in this behalf, report in person to such authority and at such time and place as may be specified in the notice.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A person who has reported in pursuance of a notice under sub-section (1) shall be enrolled in the Bangladesh Army, the Bangladesh Navy or, as the case may be, the Bangladesh Air Force unless he is, after medical examination, declared unfit for such enrolment.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) A person enrolled in a Defence Service under sub-section (2) shall, unless he is earlier discharged or released, serve in that Service until he has attained the age of thirty-five years:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that nothing in this sub-section shall be deemed-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        to prevent the retention in the Defence Service with his consent of any such person after he has attained the age of thirty-five years; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) to terminate the liability under section 6 of any such person who is discharged or released before he has attained the age of thirty-five years to be called up for refresher training every year or for service in a Defence Service.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Certificate to be granted</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. Every person-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         who has offered himself for national service in pursuance of sub-section (2) or sub-section (3) of section 3 but has not been selected for national service; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        whose liability to render national service has been deferred under section 4; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       who has been exempted from rendering national service under clause (b) or clause (c) of sub-section (2) of section 5; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv)       who has completed national service;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">shall be granted by the officer or authority prescribed in this behalf a certificate to the effect that such person has so offered himself for national service but has not been selected for such service or has been so exempted, or that his liability to render such service has been deferred for the period specified in the certificate or, as the case may be, that he has completed national service.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Permission to leave Bangladesh necessary</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. A person for the time being in Bangladesh who is liable to render national service and does not hold a certificate granted under section 9 shall not leave Bangladesh without the permission in writing of such officer or authority as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, authorise in this behalf.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Extension of age limit for competitive examinations</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. Notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force or in any rule, order or other instrument, a person who has rendered national service shall, for the purpose of appearing in any competitive examination held for appointment to any service or post, be entitled to deduct from his age the period actually spent by him in national service.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Employers not to employ certain persons</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. No employer shall employ a person who is liable to render national service unless such person holds a certificate granted under section 9.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Obligations of employers of persons in the Reserve</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. The employer of any person for the time being on the National Service Reserve who is called up for refresher training under section 7 shall, for all purposes, treat the period spent by such person in such training as period spent in the performance of duties in the service of the employer and shall not-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         terminate the services of such person while he is undergoing such training or on the ground that he is liable to be or has been called up for such training; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        make any deduction from the emoluments to which such person is entitled while on duty.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalty</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. (1) A person shall be punishable with imprisonment for a term which may extend to three years, or with fine which may extend to fifteen thousand rupees, or with both, if he-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        contravenes the provisions of sub-section (2) or sub-section (3) of section 3; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) fails to render national service when required to do so; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) fails to comply with notice under sub-section (1) of section 5; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) fails to comply with notice, or to receive training, under sub-section (1) of section 7; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) fails to comply with notice under sub-section (1) of section 8; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) contravenes the provisions of section 10; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g) contravenes the provisions of section 12; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h) contravenes the provisions of section 13.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A person who is convicted of an offence under sub-section (1) shall not be eligible to hold any office in the service of Bangladesh or any appointment in any establishment.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15. (1) The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular, and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing power, such rules may provide for all or any of the following matters, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        the manner in which and the authority to which a person liable to render national service shall offer himself for such service;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        the officers and authorities by whom notices may be issued under sub-section (1) of section 5, or sub-section (1) of section 7, or sub-section (1) of section 8;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the circumstances in which and the grounds on which a person may be exempted from the requirement of rendering national service;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        the honorarium payable to a person while rendering national service;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        the manner in which persons may be enrolled for rendering national service in any of the Defence Services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         the manner in which persons who have completed national service may be placed on the National Service Reserve;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        the nature of the training which persons on the National Service Reserve shall undergo, the period of such training, and the honorarium payable to such persons;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h) the officers and authorities by whom certificates under section 9 may be granted;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) the extent to which and the manner in which persons enrolled for rendering national service in any of the Defence Services or called up for training under sub-section (1) of section 7 shall be subject to the 6[ * * *] Army Act, 1952, the 7[ * * *] Navy Ordinance, 1961, or, as the case may be, the 8[ * * *] Air Force Act, 1953; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(j)         any other matter which may be necessary for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Jurisdiction of Courts barred</p><p style="text-align: justify;">16. No order made or proceedings taken under this Ordinance shall be called in question in any Court including the 9[ High Court Division] and the 10[ Appellate Division of the Supreme Court ].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the words “Bangladesh” and “Government” were substituted for the words “Pakistan” and “Central Government” respectively by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The word “Pakistan” was omitted Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 The words “High Court Division” were substituted for the words “High Court” by Article 7(1)(a) of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972) as amended by the Bangladesh Adaptation of Existing Laws (Amendment) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 150 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10 The words “Appellate Division of the Supreme Court” were substituted for the words “Supreme Court” by Article 7(1)(b) of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972) as amended by the Bangladesh Adaptation of Existing Laws (Amendment) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 150 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
354	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE PILOTAGE ORDINANCE, 1969 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE PILOTAGE ORDINANCE, 1969 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. V OF 1969).[6th June, 1969]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to provide for pilotage for certain vessels plying on inland waters of Bangladesh.   1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to provide for pilotage for certain vessels plying on inland waters of Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the 25th day of March, 1969, read with the Provisional Constitution Order, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the Martial Law Administrator, Zone B, performing the functions and exercising the powers of the Governor of East Pakistan, is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 2[ * * *] Pilotage Ordinance, 1969.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “Authority” means the Bangladesh Inland Water Transport Authority;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “Chairman” means the Chairman of the Authority;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) “inland water” means any canal, river or other navigable water in Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) “pilot” means a pilot of the Authority;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) “vessel” means every description of vessel ordinarily plying on inland waters and propelled wholly or in part by steam, electricity or other mechanical power, and includes a dumb barge, flat and any other craft not mechanically propelled when towed or pushed by a mechanically propelled vessel.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Certain vessels not to ply without pilot</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) A vessel not registered in Bangladesh shall not ply on any inland water without a pilot on board 3[ :</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that a vessel chartered for movement of food and relief materials may ply without such a Pilot.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A vessel registered in Bangladesh and having a hull of one hundred tons or above displacement shall not ply without a pilot on board on any inland water between-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) Chandpur and Barisal,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) Chandpur and Ilishaghat,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) Barisal and Ilishaghat, 4[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) Ilishaghat and Chittagong 5[ , and]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6[ (e)    Mongla and Jhalokati via Mongla-Ghasiakhali Canal.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Notwithstanding anything contained in sub-sections (1) and (2), the owner, the agent or the master of a vessel, which is by these sub-sections required to have a pilot on board, shall be answerable for any loss or damage caused by the vessel or by any fault of the navigation of the vessel in the same manner as he would have been if the vessel had not been so required by these sub-sections.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalty</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. If any vessel plies in contravention of section 3, the owner, the agent and the master thereof shall each be punishable with fine which may extend to five hundred rupees, or with imprisonment for a term which may extend to six months, or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Procedure</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) No Court inferior to that of a Magistrate of the first class shall try an offence under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A Court trying an offence under this Ordinance may make orders for the detention of the vessel till such time as a pilot is taken on board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) No prosecution for an offence punishable under this Ordinance shall be instituted except on a complaint made in writing by the Chairman or any person authorised by the Chairman in this behalf.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) An offence under this Ordinance may be tried in any place in which the offender may be found or which the Government, by notification in the official Gazette, appoints in this behalf or in any other place in which the offender might be tried under the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the words “Bangladesh” and “Government” were substituted for the words “East Pakistan” or “Pakistan” and “Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The colon (:) was substituted for the full stop (.) and the proviso was added thereafter by Article 2 of the Pilotage (Amendment) Order, 1973 (President's Order No. 13 of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “and” was omitted by section 2 of the Pilotage (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. III of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The comma and word “, and” was substituted for the full stop (.) by section 2 of the Pilotage (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. III of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 Clause (e) was inserted by section 2 of the Pilotage (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. III of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
355	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">   THE RAILWAY SERVANTS BENEVOLENT FUND ORDINANCE, 1969 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE RAILWAY SERVANTS BENEVOLENT FUND ORDINANCE, 1969 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. XIX OF 1969).[17th November, 1969]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to provide for the constitution of a Benevolent Fund for relief of Railway Servants and their families and matters ancillary thereto.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to provide for constitution of a Benevolent Fund for relief of Railway Servants and their families and matters ancillary thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the 25th day of March, 1969, read with Provisional Constitution Order, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the Governor is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 1[ * * *] 2[ * * *] Railway Servants Benevolent Fund Ordinance, 1969.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3[ (2) It applies to every Railway Servant.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(1)        “Board” means the Board of 4[ Trustees] of the Fund constituted under section 7 of this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2)        “Family” means,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        in the case of a male Railway Servant, wife or wives and in the case of a female Railway Servants, the husband of the Railway Servant; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        the legitimate children, step-children, parents, minor brothers and sisters of the Railway Servant residing with and wholly dependent upon him or her;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3)        “Fund” means the 5[ * * *] Railway Servants Benevolent Fund constituted under section 3 of this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) “Prescribed” means prescribed by rules made under this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7)        “Railway Servant” means,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[ (a)    a person who is a regular employee of the Railway including any one employed against temporary post and also anyone who holds any post in connection with the affairs of the Railway,]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        a Railway Servant who has retired from service but the period of his retirement from service does not exceed two years, and includes any such Railway Servants who is-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         on deputation elsewhere or on foreign service within the meaning of the 8[ * * *] Railway Establishment Code,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) undergoing study or training in or outside 9[ Bangladesh],</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       on leave,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv)       under order of suspension,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">but does not include any person employed as work-charged, casual labour and substitute, and the 10[ Director, Railway Audit] and other employees working in his office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Constitution of the Fund</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) As soon as may be after the commencement of this Ordinance, the 11[ Government] shall constitute a Fund to be known as the 12[ * * *] Railway Servants Benevolent Fund and the Fund shall vest in the Board constituted under section 7 of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Fund shall consist of,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        such grants as may, from time to time, be made by the 13[ Government],</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) Compulsory contributions received from Railway Servants at such rates as the 14[ Government] may from time to time prescribe,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) income from investments made under this Ordinance, and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        any other sum received by the Board from members of the Fund.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) All sums credited to the Fund shall be held in such custody and in such manner as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Utilisation of the Fund</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) The Fund shall be utilised for,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        the relief of the Railway Servants and their families by,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         giving financial assistance to the families of deceased Railway Servants at such rates as may be determined by the Board,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        giving financial assistance to Railway Servants invalidated out of service at such rates as may be prescribed;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        defraying expenditure incurred in respect of the management of Fund; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        such other purpose as may be prescribed from time to time.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Benefits admissible under sub-section (1) of this section shall be in addition to, not in derogation of, pensions, family pensions or gratuities, as admissible under any other law for the time being in force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Accounts and Audit</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) All contributions received under clause (b) of sub-section (2) of section 3 shall be deducted, at the source, from the salaries of the Railway Servants.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The 15[ Board] shall maintain the accounts of the Fund.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Audit of all sums credited to, and expenditure from, the Fund shall be conducted by such authority and in such manner as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. [Option to be exercised by members of All-Pakistan Service.- Omitted by section 6 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Constitution and powers of the Board</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. (1) As soon as may be after the commencement of this Ordinance, the 16[ Government] may, by notification establish a Board, to be known as the 17[ Board of Trustees of the] Railway Servants Benevolent Fund for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Board shall be a body corporate, shall be entitled to acquire and hold property and shall have perpetual succession and a common seal.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Board shall consist of a Chairman and such number of members as may be determined by the 18[ Government] and shall hold office for a term of three years.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Subject to the provisions of this Ordinance and rules made thereunder and such direction, if any, as may be issued by the 19[ Government] in this behalf, the Board shall have power to invest money credited to, and to borrow money for the Fund, and to incur expenditure therefrom for the purposes as specified in section 4.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Public Servant</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. The Chairman and members of the Board constituted under section 7 or any employee or agent appointed by the Board shall be deemed to be a Public Servant within the meaning of section 21 of the 20[ * * *] Penal Code, 1860.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Powers to recover rent and premium as arrear of land revenue</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. Any sum due as rent or premium in respect of any property owned by, and under the management of the Board, if not paid within thirty days of its having become due, may, notwithstanding anything contained in any other law, for the time being in force, be recovered as arrear of land revenue under the 21[ * * *] Public Demands Recovery Act, 1913 (Bengal Act III of 1913).</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Grounds of recovery of possession</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. Where the Board is satisfied, after making such enquiry as it thinks fit and proper, that a lessee has wilfully defaulted in payment of rent or premium, as the case may be, or that a lessee has committed an act of breach of contract, the Board may terminate the lease, after giving the lessee an opportunity of being heard, and may, by order in writing, direct such lessee to vacate the land, building or part of a building in his occupation within such period as may be specified in the order and in case he fails to vacate, provisions of the 22[ * * *] Government Lands and Buildings (Recovery of Possession) Act, 1952 (East Bengal Act X of 1952) shall mutatis mutandis apply.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Indemnity</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. No suit, prosecution or other legal proceedings shall lie in any Court against the Board or against any employee of the Board in respect of anything done or intended to be done, in good faith, under this Ordinance or rules made thereunder, or in respect of any alleged neglect or omission to perform any duty devolving upon the Board under this Ordinance, or in respect of the exercise of, or failure to exercise, any power conferred on it by this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Bar to jurisdiction of Civil Courts</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. Notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force, no Civil Court shall entertain any application or suit against the Board in respect of any property or money vested in, or owned by the Board or shall question the legality of any action taken by, or under the authority of the Board, under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. [Inapplicability of East Pakistan Ordinance No. XX of 1963.- Omitted by section 11 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. The 23[ * * *] Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The word “Eastern” was omitted by section 2 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 Sub-section (2) was substituted by section 2 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “Trustees” was substituted for the word “Management” by section 3 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “Pakistan Eastern” were omitted by section 3 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 Clauses (5) and (6) were omitted by section 3 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 Sub-clause (a) was substituted by section 3 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by section 3 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 The word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the word “Pakistan” by section 3 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10 The words and comma “Director, Railway Audit” were substituted for the words and comma “Chief Auditor, Pakistan Eastern Railway” by section 3 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">11 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Railway Board” by sections 4 and 7 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">12 The words “Pakistan Eastern” were omitted by section 4 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">13 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Railway Board” by sections 4 and 7 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">14 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Railway Board” by sections 4 and 7 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">15 The word “Board” was substituted for the words and comma “Financial Advisor and Chief Accounts Officer, Pakistan Eastern Railway” by section 4 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">16 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Railway Board” by sections 4 and 7 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">17 The words “Board of Trustees of the” were substituted for the words “Board of Management of the Pakistan Eastern” by section 7 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">18 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Railway Board” by sections 4 and 7 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">19 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Railway Board” by sections 4 and 7 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">20 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by section 8 of the Eastern Railway Servants Benevolent Fund (Amendment) Act, 1991 (Act No. IV of 1991)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">21
